<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Results of Operations and Financial Condition</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On January&#160;30, 2020, Arthur J. Gallagher&#160;&#038; Co. (the Company) issued a press release setting forth the company&#8217;s financial results for the quarter ended December&#160;31, 2019 (the Earnings Release). A copy of the Earnings Release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99.1. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

The CFO Commentary includes certain estimates relating to 2020 results. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g875231g33a76.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>NEWS RELEASE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTHUR J. GALLAGHER&nbsp;&amp; CO. ANNOUNCES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>FOURTH QUARTER AND FULL YEAR 2019 FINANCIAL RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ROLLING MEADOWS, IL, January&nbsp;30, 2020 &#151; Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co. (NYSE: AJG) today reported its financial results for the quarter and year
ended December&nbsp;31, 2019. Management will host a webcast conference call to discuss these results on Thursday, January&nbsp;30, 2020 at 5:15 p.m. ET/4:15 p.m. CT. To listen to the call, and for printer-friendly formats of this release and the
&#147;Supplemental Quarterly Data&#148; and &#147;CFO Commentary,&#148; which may also be referenced during the call, please visit <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. These documents contain both GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures.
Investors and other users of this information should read carefully the section entitled &#147;Information Regarding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; beginning on page&nbsp;10. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We had an outstanding fourth quarter to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">cap-off</FONT> an excellent full year 2019,&#148; said J.&nbsp;Patrick
Gallagher, Jr., Chairman, President and CEO. Our brokerage and risk management segments combined in fourth quarter 2019 to post: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Total revenue growth of 17%, of which 5.8% was organic revenue growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net earnings growth of 31%, EBITDAC growth of 24% and adjusted EBITDAC growth of 23%. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">We improved net earnings margin by 104&nbsp;basis points and adjusted EBITDAC margin by 134&nbsp;basis points.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">We completed 11 acquisitions with estimated annualized revenues of $117&nbsp;million. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year 2019, our results were excellent and improved over a very strong full year 2018. Our brokerage and risk management segments combined in 2019
to post: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Total revenue growth of 14%, of which 5.6% was organic revenue growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net earnings growth of 22%, EBITDAC growth of 19% and adjusted EBITDAC growth of 17%. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">We improved net earnings margin by 89&nbsp;basis points and adjusted EBITDAC margin by 76&nbsp;basis points.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">We completed 49 acquisitions with estimated annualized revenue of $468&nbsp;million. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our 2019 momentum should continue in 2020. Almost without exception, property&nbsp;&amp; casualty rates around the world are firm and continue to trend higher
in most lines and geographies. Our clients&#146; businesses are growing. Unemployment is at historically low levels nearly everywhere. This is an environment where our professionals combine their creativity and knowledge with our vast capabilities
to help clients manage risk and attract and retain talent. Further, our unique culture, guided by The Gallagher Way, continues to encourage colleagues worldwide to seek excellence for themselves, their clients, carrier partners and one another. I am
extremely pleased with our 2019 performance and excited about our future.&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(1 of 15) </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Reported fourth quarter compensation ratio was 1.4 pts lower than the same period in 2018. Adjusted fourth

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Reported fourth quarter operating expense ratio was 1.2 pts higher than the same period in 2018. Adjusted
fourth quarter operating expense ratio was 1.1 pts higher than the same period in 2018. Both ratios were primarily impacted by increased technology expenses, partially offset by savings in professional fees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Interest and banking costs and</B> <B>debt </B>- At December&nbsp;31, 2019, Gallagher had
$3,923.0&nbsp;million of borrowings from private placements, $520.0&nbsp;million of short-term borrowings under its line of credit facility and $170.6&nbsp;million outstanding under a revolving loan facility that provides funding for premium finance
receivables, which are fully collateralized by the underlying premiums held by insurance carriers, and as such are excluded from our debt covenant computations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Clean energy -</B> Consists of the operating results related to our investments in 34 clean coal production plants and royalty income from clean coal
licenses related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Chem-Mod</FONT> LLC. Additional information regarding these results is available in the &#147;CFO Commentary&#148; at <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Acquisition costs -</B> Consists mostly of external professional fees and other due diligence costs related to acquisitions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Corporate </B>-<B> </B>Consists of overhead allocations mostly related to corporate staff compensation and other corporate level activities. In addition,
this includes the tax expense related to the impact of the U.S. tax legislation passed in December 2017 - principally the partial taxation of foreign earnings, nondeductible executive compensation and entertainment expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Income Taxes </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gallagher allocates the provision for
income taxes to its Brokerage and Risk Management segments using the local country statutory rates. Gallagher&#146;s consolidated effective tax rate for the quarters ended December&nbsp;31, 2019 and 2018 was (25.7)% and (195.8)%, respectively, which
was lower than the statutory rate due to the amount of IRC Section&nbsp;45 tax credits. In fourth quarter 2019, Gallagher lowered its U.S. effective income tax rate from 26% to 25%. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Webcast Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gallagher will host a webcast
conference call on Thursday, January&nbsp;30, 2020 at 5:15 p.m. ET/4:15 p.m. CT. To listen to this call, please go to <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. The call will be available for replay at such website for at least 90 days. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Arthur J.
Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co., an international insurance brokerage and risk management services firm, is headquartered in Rolling Meadows, Illinois, has operations in 49 countries and offers client-service capabilities in more than 150 countries around
the world through a network of correspondent brokers and consultants. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Impact of a New Lease Accounting Standard in First Quarter 2019 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A new lease accounting standard was adopted as of January&nbsp;1, 2019, using the modified retrospective approach allowing Gallagher to initially apply the new
lease standard at the adoption date and recognize a cumulative effect adjustment to the opening balance of retained earnings in the first quarter 2019. Consequently, the reporting for the comparative prior year periods presented in 2019 will
continue to be in accordance with the previous lease guidance, including comparative disclosure requirements. The new lease accounting standard requires us to recognize lease
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">right-of-use</FONT></FONT> assets and lease liabilities on our balance sheet, which are established at the inception of a lease by computing a net present value of the future lease
payments. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Right-of-use</FONT></FONT> assets are amortized to expense, and the discount amount related to lease liabilities is accreted to expense, over the lease term. The
amortization of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">right-of-use</FONT></FONT> asset is calculated as the difference between the straight-line lease expense and the interest calculated on the lease liability. Rent
payments are applied against the lease liabilities. Adoption of the new lease standard resulted in the recording of net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">right-of-use</FONT></FONT> assets and lease liabilities of
approximately $379.6&nbsp;million and $420.3&nbsp;million, respectively, and the reclassification of net rent related asset and liabilities of $38.3&nbsp;million as of January&nbsp;1, 2019. The cumulative effect of the adoption was recognized as a
decrease to retained earnings of $2.4&nbsp;million on January&nbsp;1, 2019. There were de minimis impacts on the fourth quarter 2019 and year ended 2019 statement of earnings related to the adoption of this new lease standard. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Earnings Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>EBITDAC</B> <B>and EBITDAC margin </B>- EBITDAC is net earnings before interest, income taxes, depreciation,
amortization and the change in estimated acquisition earnout payables and EBITDAC margin is EBITDAC divided by total revenues (for the Brokerage segment) and revenues before reimbursements (for the Risk Management segment). These measures for the
Brokerage and Risk Management segments provide a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance and, for the overall business, provide a meaningful way to measure its financial performance on an ongoing basis.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EBITDAC</B> <B>and Adjusted EBITDAC Margin </B>- Adjusted EBITDAC is EBITDAC adjusted to exclude net
gains on divestitures, acquisition integration costs, workforce related charges, lease termination related charges, acquisition related adjustments and the period-over-period impact of foreign currency translation, as applicable (and for the
Corporate segment, the clean energy related adjustments described on page&nbsp;8) and Adjusted EBITDAC margin is Adjusted EBITDAC divided by total adjusted revenues (defined above). These measures for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments
provide a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance, and for the overall business are also presented to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree
of variability. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EPS and Adjusted Net Earnings</B> - Adjusted net earnings have been adjusted to exclude the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> impact of net gains on divestitures, acquisition integration costs, the impact of foreign currency translation, workforce related charges, lease termination related charges, acquisition related adjustments
(and for the Corporate segment, the clean energy related adjustments described on page&nbsp;8) and effective income tax rate impact described on pages 3 and 8. Adjusted EPS is Adjusted Net Earnings divided by diluted weighted average shares
outstanding. This measure provides a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance (and as such should not be used as a measure of Gallagher&#146;s liquidity), and for the overall business is also presented to improve the
comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Organic
Revenues (a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure)</B> - For the Brokerage segment, organic change in base commission and fee revenues, supplemental revenues and contingent revenues exclude the first twelve months of such revenues
generated from acquisitions and such revenues related to divested operations in each year presented.&nbsp;These revenues are excluded from organic revenues in order to help interested persons analyze the revenue growth associated with the operations
that were a part of Gallagher in both the current and prior period.&nbsp;In addition, organic change in base commission and fee revenues, supplemental revenues and contingent revenues exclude the period-over-period impact of foreign currency
translation. For the Risk Management segment, organic change in fee revenues excludes the first twelve months of fee revenues generated from acquisitions and the fee revenues related to operations disposed of in each year presented. In addition,
change in organic growth excludes the period-over-period impact of foreign currency translation to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability or are due to
the limited-time nature of these revenue sources. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These revenue items are excluded from organic revenues in order to determine a comparable, but <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP,</FONT> measurement of revenue growth that is associated with the revenue sources that are expected to continue in the current year and beyond.&nbsp;Gallagher has historically viewed organic revenue growth as an
important indicator when assessing and evaluating the performance of its Brokerage and Risk Management segments.&nbsp;Gallagher also believes that using this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure allows readers of our financial
statements to measure, analyze and compare the growth from its Brokerage and Risk Management segments in a meaningful and consistent manner. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Information Presented to GAAP Measures</B> - This press release includes tabular
reconciliations to the most comparable GAAP measures, as follows: for EBITDAC (on pages&nbsp;12 and 13), for adjusted revenues, adjusted EBITDAC and adjusted diluted net earnings per share (on pages 3 and 4), for organic revenue measures (on
pages&nbsp;5 and 6, respectively, for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments), for adjusted compensation and operating expenses and adjusted EBITDAC margin (on pages 5, 6 and 7, respectively, for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments). </P>
